				any_country = {

country_event = {
	id = rab_talk_queen.303
	title = "rab_talk_queen.NAME303"
	
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			NOT = { 
				any_owned_province = {
					has_province_modifier = quarantined_influenza
				}
			}	
			NOT = {
				any_owned_province = {
						has_province_modifier = influenza
				}			
			}
		}
		desc = "rab_talk_queen.DESC303.a"
	}	

	desc = {
		trigger = {
				any_owned_province = {
					has_province_modifier = quarantined_influenza
				}
			NOT = {
				any_owned_province = {
						has_province_modifier = influenza
				}			
			}
		}
		desc = "rab_talk_queen.DESC303.b"
	}

			NOT = { 
				any_owned_province = {

		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					check_variable = {
						which = num_of_tianshanlotus
						value = 3
					}	
				}
			}

		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "rab_talk_queen.OPTA307" #)YqS??
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					any_province = {
						has_province_modifier = md_tianshanlotus
					}
				}
				has_country_flag = flg_less_tianshanlotus		
			}
			random_province = {
				limit = {
					region = tibet_region 
				}
				add_province_modifier = {
					name = "md_tianshanlotus"
						duration = 365
				}	
				save_global_event_target_as = gt_pov_tianshanlotus
				set_province_flag = flg_tianshanlotus
				# ==> must clear the global event target when modifier end
				#rab_ need notice it must in hidden_event.121 
			}
			save_global_event_target_as = finder_tianshanlotus_tag
			clr_country_flag = flg_less_tianshanlotus
		}
		country_event = {
			id =  rab_talk_queen.1000
		}		
	}

	# self country has not the flag
	# other country has not the flag
	# flag not yet show in any province
	
	desc = {
		# stopwarflag on other country has least one
		trigger = {
			NOT = { 
				check_variable = {
					which = num_of_milbook
					value = 1
				}
			}
			NOT = {
				any_country = {
					check_variable = {
						which = num_of_milbook
						value = 1
					}					
				}

				any_province = {

				has_global_flag = flg_milbook_1limit

				has_global_flag = flg_milbook_3limit

		}

	title = "rab_talk_queen.NAME310"
	# self country has not the flag
	# other country has not the flag
	# flag not yet show in any province
	
	desc = {
		# stopwarflag on other country has least one
		trigger = {
			NOT = { 
				check_variable = {
					which = num_of_admbook
					value = 1
				}
			}
			NOT = {
				any_country = {
					check_variable = {
						which = num_of_admbook

					}

				any_province = {

country_event = {
	id = rab_talk_queen.311
	title = "rab_talk_queen.NAME311"
	desc = {
		# ≥PWâsÀt(WÍÅ∂R
		trigger = {
			has_country_modifier = md_chuanguoyuxi
			has_reform = celestial_empire
		}
		desc = "rab_talk_queen.DESC311.a"
	}
	desc = {
		# ≥PWâsÀt(WÍÅ∂R
		trigger = {
			has_country_modifier = md_chuanguoyuxi
			NOT = { has_reform = celestial_empire }
		}
		desc = "rab_talk_queen.DESC311.aa"
	}	
	desc = {
		#≥PWâsÀtN(WÍÅ∂R
		#≥PWâsÀt(W%R∂R0
		trigger = {
			NOT = { has_country_modifier = md_chuanguoyuxi }
			any_country = {
				has_country_modifier = md_chuanguoyuxi	
			}	
		}
		desc = "rab_talk_queen.DESC311.b"
	}
	desc = {	
		#≥PWâsÀtN(WÍÅ∂R
		#≥PWâsÀtN(W%R∂R0
		trigger = {
			NOT = { has_country_modifier = md_chuanguoyuxi }

	option = {
		name = "rab_talk_queen.OPTB311"
		#≥PWâsÀtN(WÍÅ∂R
		#≥PWâsÀt(W%R∂R0

#################From random event .5060 if consort has more 3 points in adm
country_event = {
	id = rab_talk_queen.1003
	title = "rab_talk_queen.NAME1003"
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			NOT = { has_reform = celestial_empire	}
		}	
		desc = "rab_talk_queen.DESC1003.a"		
	}
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			has_reform = celestial_empire
		}	
		desc = "rab_talk_queen.DESC1003.b"		
	}
	
	picture = {
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = flg_has_concert_pic1
		}
		picture = CHOICES_QUEENS_1_eventPicture 
	}
